<time>1397319944331< /time><resp>None<//resp>< Text>
Finally, after years of owning pets and taking them to different vets, I have found a place that truly cares about your pet. Not only is Dr. Rozsa the most caring, warm and loving veterinarian you will ever meet but her staff members are exactly like her.

You are always greeted warmly when you arrive and they seem genuinely happy to see you. You are also always greeted by their two "guard" cats who will quickly offer you their backs for your petting pleasure.

I had a Chihuahua that hated everybody and taking her to any vet was a nightmare.
But here, not only were they were able to groom her, but she actually started to become attached to the staff, especially Emily. When my Chihuahua was killed by two pitbulls, the staff did everything they could to help me get through it. I was so distraught over the incident that I suffered a heart attack and was hospitalized. They came to my house to pick up my pet's body and made arrangements for her cremation. I could not have made it without their loving support.

Dr Rosza truly is a vet who loves animals. She hugs and kisses my pets when they come to see her. She is so gentle with them and she clearly explains what she is doing and why, so you have a clear understanding on what is going on with your pets health.

Yesterday I had to put my beloved Dalamatian down and Dr. Rosza was extremely gentle with my dog. She explained every step of the process as she was doing it and my dog went through it with no stress or anxiety. It was a peaceful passing, unlike an experience I had gone through with another vet who sent another one of my dogs into a panic attack as she was dying.

Dr. Rosza and her staff are the best ever. I'm luck to have found them.

You can tell that Dr. Rosza truly loves animals. She even kisses and hugs my little Chihuahua. explains clearly what ailment my pet is suffering from and her recommendations.<//Text>

This cell-phone and other-device repair shop is my first choice for needed work.  When my phone needed a replacement for a severely cracked screen, the proprietor not only estimated the cost to replace the screen, but confirmed the need for a new battery.

My family needs pan dulce everyday while here visiting me so my uncle went every 2 days to get some. <Review>I've been coming here for 30 plus years. Always consistent wonderful food for a cheap price. Breakfast is a favorite! Hamburger patty and eggs are my breakfast favorite. Biscuit and gravy are always delicious! Giant Cottage burger is my lunch fave. Huge patty on a homemade roll. I order it without the Ortega chili and add mushrooms for a swiss mushroom burger. So tasty and huge. Bring your appetite!

They have changed owners from David to the employees that have worked there forever. They have kept the same great menu, but are adding some Latin dishes like posole and menudo on the weekends. I recently broke away from my hamburger patty and eggs and tried the menudo. So good!

If you're in Desert Hot Springs,  you must try this little gem. Be careful Sunday mornings as it is really packed! And make sure to make it by 1:30 because they close promptly.

Best service by Adrianna (now owner) and her daughters! I don't even have to tell them what I want to order as they have it memorized.

Every day lunch specials, but I always order the same things. Get here as soon as you can!< /Review><Pics>None< /Pics>< response>

<review>First time here with the family. Found in a Google maps search "cafe."  Impressed with the 4.4 star avg rating, as it peaked my interest compared with the quality rating of other diners and cafes across the entire Coachell Valley.

I think we have finally found the "breakfast spot" we have been searching for for 3 years since moving out here. You know, the type of place you could see yourself just ordering an appetizing yet simple plate of eggs, toast and jam with a cup of hot coffee and it not cost an arm and a leg... and it makes you happy and relaxed.

Service was fast. Employees kind and pleasantly genuine. Food was the right price for my wallet. Coffee was decent and served in a huge mug so I didn't have to keep having it refilled... which was very nice. I had the French Toast breakfast special and added a side of hashed browns. Everything was cooked and presented as I'd ordered and I'm very pleased. My husband ordered the full order of Biscuits and Gravy. While it wasn't bad, and I'd tried a bite, we both agreed it needed to be a tad more savory in flavor aside from the pepper. It was a large plate and husband was happy that it had a liberal amount of gravy to sop up. The bacon he added on the side was cooked perfectly also.

While the seating and table were clean, the silverware spotless, and the condiments generally free of food residues, the table topper signage (has the specials on it) needs some love. It was kind of gross especially since it's probably one of the first things patrons will touch at the table. But it is an easily rectified issue, so no biggie in the end for me.

All in all, it was a wonderful experience and atmosphere. I was very satisfied with the prices and the general quality of the meals. I will come back... most likely/maybe make this my family's weekend breakfast tradition.<//review>< pictures>
